<h1><strong><a id="Security_Roles_and_Descriptions"></a><a id="Top"></a>Security Roles and Descriptions</strong></h1>
<p>When deciding which security levels to use, please consider the following:</p>
<p style="margin-left: 40px;">Although assigning a role to an employee is important in terms of security, it is more important to look at what the role the employee is assigned has set for a specific screen or form in question. Use the <strong>Security Screen Setup</strong> to do this.</p>
<h1><a id="ScreenToolTips"></a><span style="color: #000000;">Security Screen Tool Tips </span></h1>
<p>We have added some <strong>Screen Tools</strong> to help you make sense of this screen</p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><img src="http://iqmetrix.helpdocsonline.com/userfiles/569/1857/ckfinder/images/2014_09_04_13_58_34.png?dc=201409041357-105" data-cke-saved-src="http://iqmetrix.helpdocsonline.com/userfiles/569/1857/ckfinder/images/2014_09_04_13_58_34.png?dc=201409041357-105" /></p>
<p>You will see three vertical dots <img src="http://iqmetrix.helpdocsonline.com/userfiles/569/1857/ckfinder/images/icons%20and%20stock%20images/More-Grid.png?dc=201412231034-1" alt="" data-cke-saved-src="/userfiles/569/1857/ckfinder/images/icons%20and%20stock%20images/More-Grid.png?dc=201412231034-1" /> on some pages, click these dots to see the <strong>Save As</strong>, <strong>Email</strong>, <strong>Copy to Clipboard</strong>, <strong>Print</strong> and <strong>Text Size</strong> options.</p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><img src="http://iqmetrix.helpdocsonline.com/userfiles/569/1857/ckfinder/images/2014_09_04_14_01_34.png?dc=201409041400-107" data-cke-saved-src="http://iqmetrix.helpdocsonline.com/userfiles/569/1857/ckfinder/images/2014_09_04_14_01_34.png?dc=201409041400-107" /></p>
<p>You will also see a circle with a blue "i" in it. This is a tool tip that will help you understand what something means. Click on it for various explanations and tips.</p>
<p style="text-align: center;"><img src="http://iqmetrix.helpdocsonline.com/userfiles/569/1857/ckfinder/images/2014_09_04_14_04_16.png?dc=201409041403-105" data-cke-saved-src="http://iqmetrix.helpdocsonline.com/userfiles/569/1857/ckfinder/images/2014_09_04_14_04_16.png?dc=201409041403-105" /></p>
<p>Some <strong>Setup Screens</strong> have screen selectors. From here, you can quickly navigate to other setup screens that are related to the one you currently have open.</p>
<h1><a id="Security_Screen_Setup"></a>Security Screen Setup</h1>
<p><strong>Settings Console | Employees | Security Screen Setup</strong><br /> <strong>Settings Console | </strong>search <strong>| Security Screen Setup</strong></p>
<p><span style="color: #0000ff;"><strong>NOTE:</strong></span> <em>you may also use the drop down to select <strong>Security Screen Setup</strong> from <strong>Security Role Setup</strong></em></p>
<p>The <strong>Security Screen Setup </strong>allows you to set specific security levels for each employee role and module within the system. It allows you to control what each employee role sees or doesn't see; what they can and cannot do within RQ.</p>
<p><img src="http://iqmetrix.helpdocsonline.com/userfiles/569/1857/ckfinder/images/2015_07_21_18_48_213.png?dc=201507211846-49" data-cke-saved-src="/userfiles/569/1857/ckfinder/images/2015_07_21_18_48_213.png?dc=201507211846-49" /></p>
<ol>
<li>Select the <strong>Security Setting </strong>you would like to add or edit security for by scrolling through the list of settings on the left, or type the name of the setting in the search box</li>
<li>Highlight your selection in the left pane</li>
<li>In the role chosen, click the drop down menu under <strong>Security Description</strong></li>
<li>Choose the<strong> Security Level </strong>from the drop down menu, see the <strong>Security Roles</strong> and <strong>Descriptions</strong> below for information on selecting an appropriate level</li>
<li>Determine if you would like each role <strong>Visible </strong>or not. If a <strong>Security Screen</strong> is made visible for a <strong>Security Role</strong>, any user with that role can edit it for all accessible roles.</li>
</ol>
<p><img src="http://iqmetrix.helpdocsonline.com/userfiles/569/1857/ckfinder/images/Assigned%20Security%20Level%201.jpg?dc=201503121751-0" alt="" data-cke-saved-src="/userfiles/569/1857/ckfinder/images/Assigned%20Security%20Level%201.jpg?dc=201503121751-0" /></p>
<ol start="6">
<li>Continue this process for each <strong>Security Role </strong>for the screen chosen. You can choose to edit each line individually, or select multiple lines and choose to apply <strong>For Selected</strong>, or <strong>For All</strong>.</li>
</ol>
<p><img src="http://iqmetrix.helpdocsonline.com/userfiles/569/1857/ckfinder/images/Assigned%20Security%20Level%202.jpg?dc=201503121751-0" alt="" data-cke-saved-src="/userfiles/569/1857/ckfinder/images/Assigned%20Security%20Level%202.jpg?dc=201503121751-0" /></p>
<ul style="margin-left: 40px;">
<li>Use the drop down under <strong>Set: </strong>to determine if you would like to change <strong>Security Description</strong> or <strong>Visible,</strong> then use the drop down under <strong>To</strong>: to determine selected security description, or check <strong>Visible</strong></li>
</ul>
<ol start="7">
<li>Click the <strong>Cancel </strong>button on the top toolbar if you wish to cancel your current transaction. You will be prompted with the following message: "Security Screen Setup All changes made will be cancelled. Are you sure?". Click <strong>Yes</strong> to continue, or <strong>No</strong> to Cancel.</li>
<li>You can filter each <strong>Security Screen</strong> by <strong>Security Description</strong> to assist you in identifying which <strong>Security Role</strong> has a particular description</li>
<li>Once complete, click <strong>Save</strong></li>
<li>Repeat the above steps for each screen you need to change</li>
</ol>
<h1><strong><a id="AR_Accounts_Receivable_Security_Settings"></a>A/R (Accounts Receivable) Security Settings</strong></h1>
<p><a href="#AR_AR_Master_List">A/R: A/R Master List</a><br /> <a href="#AR_New_Account">A/R: New Account</a><br /> <a href="#AR_Pay_Off_Account">A/R: Pay Off Account</a><br /> <a href="#AR_Update_Account">A/R: Update Account</a></p>
<p><a id="AR_AR_Master_List"></a><u><strong>A/R: A/R Master List</strong></u></p>
<p><em>Reports Console | Utilities | Accounts Receivable Master List</em></p>
<p><em><strong>Full Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>access all functions available to this screen</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>No Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>access is denied</li>
<li>message will display, "You do not have security clearance"</li>
</ul>
<p>For details on <strong>Full Access </strong>see <a href="https://support.iqmetrix.com/hc/en-us/articles/229126948#Accounts_Receivable_Master_List">Accounts Receivable Master List</a></p>
<p><a id="AR_New_Account"></a><u><strong>A/R: New Account</strong></u></p>
<p><em>Finance Console | Accounts Receivable | New A/R Account</em></p>
<p><em><strong>Full Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>access all functions available to this screen</li>
<li>create new A/R accounts</li>
<li>view G/L A/R Control Account</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>Restricted Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>create new A/R accounts</li>
<li>G/L A/R Control Account is hidden</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>No Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>access is denied</li>
<li>message will display, "You do not have security clearance"</li>
</ul>
<p>For details on <strong>Full Access </strong>see <a href="https://support.iqmetrix.com/hc/en-us/articles/229063488#Creating_A_New_Customer_Account">Creating A New Customer Account</a></p>

<p><a id="AR_Update_Account"></a><u><strong>A/R: Update Account</strong></u></p>
<p><em>Finance Console | Accounts Receivable | Update A/R Account</em></p>
<p><em><strong>Full Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>access all functions available to this screen</li>
<li>view G/L A/R Control Account</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>Restricted Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>update accounts</li>
<li>G/L A/R Control Account is hidden</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>View Only</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>G/L A/R Control Account is hidden</li>
<li>unable to update accounts</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>No Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>access is denied</li>
<li>message will display, "You do not have security clearance"</li>
</ul>

<h1><strong><a id="Cash_Management_Security_Settings"></a>Cash Management Security Settings</strong></h1>
<p><a href="#Cash_Management_Cash_Alerts">Cash Management: Cash Alerts</a><br /> <a href="#Cash_Management_Close_Out_Drawer">Cash Management: Close Out Drawer</a><br /> <a href="#Cash_Management_Drawer_Audit">Cash Management: Drawer Audit</a><br /> <a href="#Cash_Management_Force_Cash_Skim">Cash Management: Force Cash Skim</a><br /> <a href="#Cash_Management_New_Cash_Skim">Cash Management: New Cash Skim</a><br /> <a href="#Cash_Management_New_Cash_In">Cash Management: New Cash-In</a><br /> <a href="#Cash_Management_New_MultiDrawer_Cashout">Cash Management: New Multi-Drawer Cashout</a><br /> <a href="#Cash_Management_New_Single_Drawer_Cashout">Cash Management: New Single-Drawer Cashout</a><br /> <a href="#Cash_Management_Reconcile_Cashouts">Cash Management: Reconcile Cashouts</a></p>
<p><a id="Cash_Management_Cash_Alerts"></a><u><strong>Cash Management: Cash Alerts</strong></u></p>
<p><em>Sales Console | Cash Management</em></p>
<p><em><strong>Always Show Alerts</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>alerted whenever there is a discrepancy between the <strong>Your Total </strong>amount and the <strong>System Total </strong>amount</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>Show Alerts If Under</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>only alerted if the <strong>Your Total</strong> amount is lower than the <strong>System Total</strong> amount</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>Never Show Alerts</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>never alerted when there are discrepancies between the <strong>Your Total</strong> amount and the <strong>System Total</strong> amount</li>
</ul>
<p><span style="line-height: 1.6em;"><span style="color: #0000ff;"><strong>NOTE</strong></span>: </span><em style="line-height: 1.6em;">the alerts are attached to the setting in the <strong>Settings Console | Company Settings | Finance | Allowable Variance Amount for Blind Cashouts</strong>. This is where you set that amount, anything over that variance will trigger an alerts for both <strong>Always Show Alerts</strong> and <strong>Show Alerts If Under</strong></em></p>
<p>For settings details see <a href="https://support.iqmetrix.com/hc/en-us/articles/228837807-Settings-Company-Settings#Finance">Company Settings</a></p>
<p><a id="Cash_Management_Close_Out_Drawer"></a><u><strong>Cash Management: Close Out Drawer</strong></u></p>
<p><em>Sales Console | Cash Management | Close Drawer</em></p>
<p><em><strong>Full Access </strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>access all functions available to this screen including:</li>
<ul>
<li><strong>Over (Short) </strong>value above<strong> Total </strong>is visible</li>
<li><strong>Select Terminals </strong>screen</li>
<ul>
<li><strong>Cash In Amount</strong> column is visible</li>
<li><strong>Till Transactions</strong> column is visible</li>
</ul>
<li><strong>Count Cash </strong>screen</li>
<ul>
<li><strong>The expected amount in your drawer is $xx.xx</strong> is visible</li>
</ul>
<li><strong>Count Non-Cash</strong> screen</li>
<ul>
<li><strong>Systems Total</strong> column is visible</li>
<li><strong>Difference</strong> column is visible</li>
</ul>
</ul>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>Blind Close Drawer</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li><strong>Over (Short) </strong>value above<strong> Total </strong>is hidden</li>
<ul>
<li><strong>Select Terminals </strong>screen</li>
<li><strong>Cash In Amount</strong> column is hidden</li>
<li><strong>Till Transactions</strong> column is hidden</li>
</ul>
<li><strong>Count Cash </strong>screen</li>
<ul>
<li><strong>The expected amount in your drawer is $xx.xx</strong> is hidden</li>
</ul>
<li><strong>Count Non-Cash</strong> screen</li>
<ul>
<li><strong>Systems Total</strong> column is hidden</li>
<li><strong>Difference</strong> column is hidden</li>
</ul>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>No Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>access is denied</li>
<li>message will display, "You do not have security clearance"</li>
</ul>
<p>For details on <strong>Full Access</strong> see <a href="https://support.iqmetrix.com/hc/en-us/articles/229127008#Close_Drawer_Multi_Drawer">Close Drawer (Multi-Drawer)</a></p>
<p><a id="Cash_Management_Drawer_Audit"></a><u><strong>Cash Management: Drawer Audit</strong></u></p>
<p><em>Sales Console | Cash Management | Drawer Audit</em></p>
<p><em><strong>Full Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>

</ul>
<p><em><strong>No Access</strong></em></p>

<p><a id="Cash_Management_Force_Cash_Skim"></a><u><strong>Cash Management: Force Cash Skim</strong></u></p>
<p><em>Operations Console | Location Setup | Financial</em></p>
<p><em><strong>Full Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>will see skim alert</li>
<li>able to use login credentials to bypass the alert, and process a sale <u>without</u> completing a cash skim</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>No Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>requires you to complete a cash skim when prompted</li>
</ul>
<p>For details on <strong>Full Access</strong> see <a href="https://support.iqmetrix.com/hc/en-us/articles/229127248-Settings-Company#Financial_Details">Location Setup</a></p>

<p><em>Sales Console | Cash Management | New Cash-In</em></p>
<p><em><strong>Full Access</strong></em></p>

<p><a id="Cash_Management_New_MultiDrawer_Cashout"></a><u><strong>Cash Management: New Multi-Drawer Cashout</strong></u></p>
<p><em>Sales Console | Cash Management | New Cashout</em></p>
<p><em><strong>Full Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>access all functions available to this screen</li>
<li>view/edit all fields</li>
<li>add comments</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>Blind Cashout</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>enforces maximum allowable cashout variance</li>
<li>unable to view <strong>Over (Short)</strong> balance</li>
<li><strong>Cashout Details</strong> toolbar button hidden (unable to view Transaction Inquiry Report)</li>
<li>unable to add comments</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>No Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>unable to open <strong>New Cashout</strong> screen</li>
<li>message will display: "You do not have security clearance"</li>
</ul>
<p>For details on <strong>Full Access </strong>see <a href="https://support.iqmetrix.com/hc/en-us/articles/229127008-Sales-Console#New_Cashout_Multi_Drawer">New Multi-Drawer </a><a href="#New_Cashout_Multi_Drawer">Cashout</a></p>

<p><em><strong>Full Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>access all functions available to this screen</li>
<li>view/edit all fields</li>
<li>add comments</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>Blind Cashout</strong></em></p>
<ul>

<li>unable to add comments</li>

<p><em><strong>No Access</strong></em></p>

<li>message will display: "You do not have security clearance"</li>

<h1><a id="Console_Security_Settings"></a><strong>Console Security Settings</strong></h1>
<p><a href="#Console_Employees">Console: Employees</a><br /> <a href="#Console_Finance">Console: Finance</a><br /> <a href="#Console_Operations">Console: Operations</a><br /> <a href="#Console_Sales">Console: Sales</a></p>
<p><a id="Console_Employees"></a><strong><u>Console: Employees</u></strong></p>
<p><em><strong>Full Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>access all functions available to this console</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>Restricted Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>provides access to the console with the restrictions below</li>
<li><strong>General</strong>:</li>
</ul>
<ul>
<ul>
<li>can view all non-hidden fields</li>
<li>can edit subordinate employees' <strong>Name</strong>, <strong>Address</strong>, <strong>Phone Numbers</strong>, <strong>SMS </strong>and <strong>Personal Email </strong>fields</li>
<li>can edit <u>own</u> <strong>Password</strong>, <strong>Passphrase </strong>(if applicable) and <strong>Email Password </strong>fields</li>
<li><strong>Comments </strong>hidden</li>
</ul>
</ul>
<ul>
<li><strong>Activities</strong>:</li>
</ul>
<ul>
<ul>
<li>can view but not open <strong>Activities </strong>for other employees</li>
<li>can view but not open own <strong>Activities</strong></li>
<li>cannot create new <strong>Activities</strong> for other employees</li>
</ul>
</ul>
<ul>
<li><strong>Admin</strong>:</li>
</ul>
<ul>
<ul>
<li>hidden</li>
</ul>
</ul>
<ul>
<li><strong>Documents</strong></li>
</ul>
<ul>
<ul>
<li>can view, open and delete subordinate employees' <strong>Documents</strong></li>
<li>cannot upload <strong>Documents</strong></li>
</ul>
</ul>
<ul>
<li><strong>Groups</strong>:</li>
</ul>
<ul>
<ul>
<li>can view other employees' <strong>Groups</strong></li>
<li>cannot add other employees to <strong>Groups</strong></li>
</ul>
</ul>
<ul>
<li><strong>Integration</strong>:</li>
</ul>
<ul>
<ul>
<li>hidden</li>
</ul>
</ul>
<ul>
<li><strong>Locations:</strong></li>
</ul>
<ul>
<ul>
<li>can view other employees' <strong>Locations</strong></li>
<li>cannot add other employees to or remove them from <strong>Locations</strong></li>
</ul>
</ul>
<ul>
<li><strong>Time Off</strong>:</li>
</ul>
<ul>
<ul>
<li>can <strong>Assign RTO</strong></li>
</ul>
</ul>
<ul>
<li><strong>Work History</strong>:</li>
</ul>
<ul>
<ul>
<li>hidden</li>
</ul>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>No Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>access is denied</li>
<li>icon does not appear on the user's home screen</li>
</ul>
<p>For details on <strong>Full Access</strong> see <a href="https://support.iqmetrix.com/hc/en-us/articles/228695067-Employee-Console">Employees Console</a></p>
<p><a id="Console_Finance"></a><u><strong>Console: Finance</strong></u></p>
<p><em><strong>Full Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>access all functions available to this console</li>
<li>access to <strong>Process Metrix</strong></li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>Restricted Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>access to the console but additional access within the <strong>Finance Console </strong>will depend on the security settings for those features</li>
<li>unable to view <strong>Process Metrix</strong> (button is there but will not load)</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>No Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>access is denied</li>
<li>icon does not appear on the user's home screen</li>
</ul>
<p>For details on <strong>Full Access</strong> see <a href="https://support.iqmetrix.com/hc/en-us/articles/229063488-Finance-Console">Finance Console</a></p>
<p><a id="Console_Operations"></a><u><strong>Console: Operations</strong></u></p>
<p><em><strong>Full Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>access all functions available to this console</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>View Own Region</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>view locations/employees in own region</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>View Own District</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>view locations/employees in own district</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>View Own Location</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>view employees in own location</li>
</ul>

<ul>
<li>view own profile</li>
</ul>
<p>For details on <strong>Full Access</strong> see <a href="https://support.iqmetrix.com/hc/en-us/articles/228828767">Operations Console</a></p>
<p><a id="Console_Sales"></a><u><strong>Console: Sales</strong></u><br />
(this setting replaced <strong>POS: Sales Console</strong>)</p>
<p><em><strong>Full Access </strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>access all functions available to this console</li>
<li><strong>Quick Sale</strong> is enabled</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>Force Customer On New Sale</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>access all functions available to this console excluding <strong>Quick Sale</strong></li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>No Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>access is denied</li>
<li>icon does not appear on the user's home screen</li>
</ul>
<p>For details on <strong>Full Access</strong> see <a href="https://support.iqmetrix.com/hc/en-us/articles/229127008">Sales Console</a></p>

<p><a id="CRM_Customer_View"></a><u><strong>CRM: Customer View</strong></u></p>
<p><em>Customers Console | Search Customers | select customer</em></p>
<p><em><strong>Full Access </strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>access all functions available this screen</li>
<li>relationships are visible</li>
<li>can set customers as tax exempt and see tax exemptions grid</li>
<li>multi-level pricing enabled</li>
<li>custom fields are visible</li>
<li>notes are visible and editable</li>
<li>can see web password text box</li>
<li>can toggle <strong>Accept Checks</strong> or <strong>Accept Cheques</strong></li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>Update Customers, No Setting Customer Identifiers, No Setting Tax Exemptions, No Setting Pricing Groups</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>can edit notes</li>
<li>can view <strong>Customer Identifier</strong> but not edit</li>
<li>unable to set customers as tax exempt or see tax exemptions grid</li>
<li>multi-level pricing is disabled</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>Update Customers, No Viewing Customer Identifiers, No Setting Tax Exemptions, No Setting Pricing Groups</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>can view notes but not edit</li>
<li><strong>Customer Identifier</strong> is hidden</li>
<li>unable to set customers as tax exempt or see tax exemptions grid</li>
<li>multi-level pricing is disabled</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>View Only</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>can view but not edit</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>No Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>access is denied</li>
<li>message will display, "You do not have security clearance"</li>
</ul>
<p>For details on <strong>Full Access</strong> see <a href="https://support.iqmetrix.com/hc/en-us/articles/229062948-Customers-Console#Creating_New_Customers_Editing_Existing_Customers">Creating / Editing Customers</a></p>

<li>unable to delete documents</li>
</ul>

<li>unable to view or delete documents</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>View Only</strong></em></p>

<li>can view documents</li>
<li>unable to add or delete documents</li>
</ul>

<p><a id="CRM_iQmanager"></a><u><strong>CRM: iQmanager</strong></u></p>
<p><em>Operations Console | iQmanager</em></p>
<p><em><strong>Full Access </strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li><span style="line-height: 1.6em;">access all functions available to this screen</span></li>
<li>view data for any company tree element as well as any node in the iQmanager search tree</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>View Your Own Region</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>view data for any company tree node for regions to which the employee is assigned and nodes beneath</li>
<li>access to own tasks, messages, time sheets and employee activities</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>View Your Own District</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>access to view data for any company tree node for districts to which the employee is assigned and nodes beneath</li>
<li>access to own tasks, messages, time sheets and employee activities</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>View Your Own Location</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>access to view data for any company tree node for locations to which the employee is assigned and nodes beneath</li>
<li>access to own tasks, messages, time sheets and employee activities</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>View Yourself Only</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>access to own tasks, messages, time sheets and employee activities</li>
</ul>
<p>For further details see <a href="https://support.iqmetrix.com/hc/en-us/articles/228829127-iQmanager#Overview">iQmanager Overview</a></p>

<p><a id="CRM_Update_Sales_Opportunity"></a><u><strong>CRM: Update Sales Opportunity</strong></u></p>
<p><em>Customers Console | Customer Profile | Opportunities</em></p>
<p><em><strong>Full Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>access all functions available to this screen</li>
<li>able to Email</li>
<li>able to create new Activity</li>
<li>able to select Opportunity type</li>
<li>able to select Location</li>
<li>able to assign Sales Opportunity</li>
<li>able to edit Contact Name</li>
<li>able to edit Contact #</li>
<li>able to select Description</li>
<li>able to edit Comments</li>
<li>able to select Sales Stage</li>
</ul>
<p><strong><em>View All, Update Your Own Only</em></strong><br />
<strong><span style="color: #0000ff;">NOTE</span>: </strong><em>"own" is defined as assigned to the user, not created by the user</em></p>
<ul>
<li>able to view all Sales Opportunities</li>
<li>able to Email own Sales Opportunities</li>
<li>able to create new Activity for own Sales Opportunities</li>
<li>able to select Opportunity type for own Sales Opportunities</li>
<li>able to select Location for own Sales Opportunities</li>
<li>able to assign own Sales Opportunity</li>
<li>able to edit Contact Name for own Sales Opportunities</li>
<li>able to edit Contact # for own Sales Opportunities</li>
<li>able to select Description for own Sales Opportunities</li>
<li>able to edit Comments for own Sales Opportunities</li>
<li>able to select Sales Stage for own Sales Opportunities</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>View Only</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>able to view all sales opportunities</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>View Own Only</strong></em><br />
<strong><span style="color: #0000ff;">NOTE</span>: </strong><em>"own" is defined as assigned to the user, not created by the user</em></p>
<ul>
<li>able to view own but unable to edit anything</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>No Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>access is denied</li>
<li>message will display, "You do not have security clearance"</li>
</ul>

<h1><a id="Fingerprint_Security_Settings"></a>Fingerprint Security Settings</h1>
<p><a href="#Fingerprint_Enroll_User_Fingerprint_Templates">Fingerprint: Enroll User Fingerprint Templates</a><br /> <a href="#Fingerprint_Login_Authentication">Fingerprint: Login Authentication</a><br /> <a href="#Fingerprint_Punch_in_Authentication">Fingerprint: Punch-in Authentication</a><br /> <a href="#Fingerprint_Workstation_Hardware_Override">Fingerprint: Workstation Hardware Override</a></p>
<p><a id="Fingerprint_Enroll_User_Fingerprint_Templates"></a><u><strong>Fingerprint: Enroll User Fingerprint Templates</strong></u></p>
<p><em>Employees Console | Employee Profile | General | Security</em></p>
<p><em><strong>Full Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>update/enroll any fingerprint</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>No Access</strong></em></p>

<li>unable to update/enroll any fingerprint</li>
</ul>
<p>For details on <strong>Full Access</strong> see <a href="https://support.iqmetrix.com/hc/en-us/articles/228695067-Employee-Console#General_Section_Security">New Employee</a><br />
For details on <strong>Full Access</strong> see <a href="https://support.iqmetrix.com/hc/en-us/articles/228837827-Settings-Workstation-Settings#Set_Up_Employee_Fingerprint_Authentication">Set Up Employee Fingerprint Authentication</a></p>
<p><a id="Fingerprint_Login_Authentication"></a><u><strong>Fingerprint: Login Authentication</strong></u></p>
<p><em>Home Console</em></p>
<p><em><strong>Fingerprint or Password</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>scan fingerprint or enter password to log in</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>Password Only</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>unable to scan fingerprint to log in</li>
<li>must enter password to log in</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>Fingerprint Only</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>unable to enter password to log in</li>
<li>must scan fingerprint to log in</li>
</ul>
<p>For more detail see <a href="https://support.iqmetrix.com/hc/en-us/articles/228764327-Getting-Started#Logging_in_Using_your_Fingerprint_Scanner">Logging In and Out</a></p>
<p><a id="Fingerprint_Punch_in_Authentication"></a><u><strong>Fingerprint: Punch-in Authentication</strong></u></p>
<p><em>Home Console | Punch Clock Widget</em><br />
<em>Operations Console | Punch Clock</em></p>
<p><em><strong>Fingerprint or Password</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>scan fingerprint or enter password to punch in</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>Password Only</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>unable to scan fingerprint to punch in</li>
<li>must enter password to punch in</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>Fingerprint Only</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>unable to enter password to punch in</li>
<li>must scan fingerprint to punch in</li>
</ul>
<p>For more detail see <a href="https://support.iqmetrix.com/hc/en-us/articles/229062568-Home-Console#Punch_Clock_Widget">Widgets</a><br />
For more detail see <a href="https://support.iqmetrix.com/hc/en-us/articles/228695067-Employee-Console#Punch_Clock">HR Scheduling</a></p>
<p><a id="Fingerprint_Workstation_Hardware_Override"></a><u><strong>Fingerprint: Workstation Hardware Override</strong></u></p>
<p><em>Settings Console | Workstation Settings | Fingerprint Scanner</em></p>
<p><em><strong>Full Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>access to check the box to override all security role defaults and allow password logins if the fingerprint scanner is missing or damaged</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>No Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>access is denied</li>
<li>message will display, "You do not have security clearance"</li>
</ul>
<p>For more detail see <a href="https://support.iqmetrix.com/hc/en-us/articles/228837827-Settings-Workstation-Settings#Fingerprint_Scanner">Workstation Settings</a></p>
<p><strong>TO SET FINGERPRINT OVERRIDE: this will allow either scanner or typed passwords to be used on a specific workstation.</strong></p>
<p><img src="http://iqmetrix.helpdocsonline.com/userfiles/569/1857/ckfinder/images/Fingerprint%20Scanner.jpg?dc=201501262048-0" alt="" data-cke-saved-src="/userfiles/569/1857/ckfinder/images/Fingerprint%20Scanner.jpg?dc=201501262048-0" /></p>
<p><strong>Security Workstation Override</strong> is an option that allows a particular workstation to allow EITHER scanner or typed passwords to be used.</p>
<p>If you do not use this option, any workstation with a fingerprint scanner installed properly will default to allow fingerprint login only</p>

<p><em>Settings Console | Company Settings | Account Security</em></p>
<p><em><strong>Full Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>toggle all Password Strength restrictions</li>
</ul>
<p><a style="margin-left: 40px;">Simple Passwords<br />
<a style="margin-left: 40px;">Complex Passwords</p>
<ul>
<li>modify the minimum password length</li>
<li>set Password Renewal option</li>
<li>set number of password revisions before a password can be reused</li>
<li>set number of password failures permitted before an employee's profile is locked</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>No Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>access is denied</li>
<li>message will display, "You do not have security clearance"</li>
</ul>

<p><a id="HR_Location_Change"></a><u><strong>H/R: Location Change</strong></u></p>
<p><em>Home Console | Login screen</em></p>
<p><em><strong>Full Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>change locations using the location drop-down list once logged in if access to <a href="#Login_Permissions">Login: Permissions</a> is set to <strong>All Locations</strong> or <strong>Assigned Locations</strong></li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>No Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>unable to change locations using the location drop-down list once logged in regardless of whether the location is an assigned location</li>
</ul>
<p><strong><span style="color: #0000ff;">NOTE</span><em>: </em></strong><em>to restrict access to changing locations using the location change drop-down list in RQ to only locations that are assigned to a particular employee, give them "Assigned Locations" access to Login: Permissions and "Full Access" permission to H/R: Location Change</em></p>
<p>For details on <strong>Full Access</strong> see <a href="https://support.iqmetrix.com/hc/en-us/articles/228764327-Getting-Started#Logging_In_and_Out">Logging In and Out</a></p>
<p><a id="HR_New_Employee"></a><u><strong>H/R: New Employee</strong></u></p>
<p><em>Employees Console | New Employee</em></p>
<p><em><strong>Full Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>access all functions available to this screen</li>
<li>create new employees</li>
<li>upload documents <u>after</u> the employee is saved</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>Restricted Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>create new employees</li>
</ul>

<h1><a id="IntraiQ_Security_Settings"></a><strong>IntraiQ Security Settings</strong></h1>
<p><a href="#IntraiQ_Approve_and_Assign_RTOs_Requested_Time_Off">IntraiQ: Approve &amp; Assign RTOs (Requested Time Off)</a><br /> <a href="#IntraiQ_Approve_Shift_Swaps">IntraiQ: Approve Shift Swaps</a><br /> <a href="#IntraiQ_Assign_Tasks">IntraiQ: Assign Tasks</a><br /> <a href="#IntraiQ_Assign_Tests">IntraiQ: Assign Tests</a><br /> <a href="#IntraiQ_Bulletin_Admin">IntraiQ: Bulletin Admin</a><br /> <a href="#IntraiQ_Create_Tests">IntraiQ: Create Tests</a><br /> <a href="#IntraiQ_Document_Manager_Admin">IntraiQ: Document Manager Admin</a><br /> <a href="#IntraiQ_Employee_Of_The_Week_Admin">IntraiQ: Employee Of The Week Admin</a><br /> <a href="#IntraiQ_Enable_Disable_Employee_Of_The_Week">IntraiQ: Enable / Disable Employee Of The Week</a><br /> <a href="#IntraiQ_Scheduling_Access">IntraiQ: Scheduling Access</a><br /> <a href="#IntraiQ_View_Company_Directory">IntraiQ: View Company Directory</a><br /> <a href="#IntraiQ_View_Employee_RTOs">IntraiQ: View Employee RTOs </a><br /> <a href="#IntraiQ_View_Store_Schedule">IntraiQ: View Store Schedule</a><br /> <a href="#IntraiQ_View_Test_Results">IntraiQ: View Test Results</a></p>
<p><strong><span style="color: #0000ff;">A quick note on the tiered security module system</span>:</strong></p>
<p>The tiered system is setup so you can specify tiers to your security</p>
<p><strong>For example:</strong> a Store Owner would have level 1 security and would be able to approve anyone's RTO. A Store Manager might only have Level 3 security, so therefore wouldn't be able to approve the store owner's RTO, but would be able to approve anyone with a level 4 or 5 security. A store clerk would have level 5 security, and therefore not be able to approve anyone's RTO.</p>
<p>This also works with assigning time off - a store manager would be able to assign time off to a store clerk but not a store owner</p>
<p><a id="IntraiQ_Approve_and_Assign_RTOs_Requested_Time_Off"></a><u><strong>IntraiQ: Approve &amp; Assign RTOs (Requested Time Off)</strong></u></p>
<p><em>Employees Console | Employee Profile | Time Off | Assign RTO</em></p>
<p><em><strong>Approve &amp; Assign All RTOs</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>approve and assign any level of RTO from anyone with any level of security</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>Approve &amp; Assign Level 3 RTOs</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>approve and assign any RTO for employees with a level 4, 5, and no access</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>Approve &amp; Assign Level 4 RTOs</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>approve and assign any RTO for employees with a level 5 and no access</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>Approve &amp; Assign Level 5 RTOs</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>approve and assign any RTO for employees with no access</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>No Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>unable to approve or assign any RTOs</li>
</ul>
<p>For details on <strong>Full Access </strong>see <a href="https://support.iqmetrix.com/hc/en-us/articles/228695067#Time_Off_Section">Editing Employee Information</a></p>

<p><em>Intranet | Scheduling</em></p>

<p><em><strong>Approve Level 3 Shift Swaps</strong></em></p>

</ul>
<p><em><strong>Approve Level 4 Shift Swaps</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>approve any Shift Swaps for employees with a level 5 and Approve Own Shift Swaps access</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>Approve Level 5 Shift Swaps</strong></em></p>

</ul>

</ul>

<p><a id="Inventory_Availability_and_System_Totals"></a><strong><u>Inventory: Availability and System Totals</u></strong></p>
<p><em>Inventory Console | Open Any Product | Availability</em></p>
<p><em><strong>Full Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>access all functions available to this screen</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>View Channel Only</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>view availability (quantity) and pricing tabs of product for the channel(s) in which the user is associated to at least one location</li>
<li>system totals will be the total within the same scope.</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>View Region Only</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>view availability (quantity) and pricing tabs of product for the region(s) in which the user is associated to at least one location</li>
<li>system totals will be the total within the same scope.</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>View District Only</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>view availability (quantity) and pricing tabs of product for the district(s) in which the user is associated to at least one location</li>
<li>system totals will be the total within the same scope.</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>View Logged in Location Only</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>view totals for own location</li>
</ul>
<p>For details on <strong>Full Access</strong> see <a href="https://support.iqmetrix.com/hc/en-us/articles/229070368-Inventory-Products#Availability">Regular Products</a></p>

<p><a id="Inventory_Inventory_Management"></a><u><strong>Inventory: Inventory Management</strong></u></p>
<p><em><strong>Full Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>access to delete any type of product</li>
<li>need Full access to be able to create a new product via the Create Similar option</li>
<li>can toggle the "Refund to Used " status</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>Restricted Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>refer to screenshot below</li>
<li>access to delete Regular Products or Gift Card Products</li>
<li>can toggle the "Refund to Used" Status</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>Full View Only</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>refer to screenshot below</li>
<li>unable to delete any products</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>Restricted View Only #1</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>refer to screenshot below</li>
<li>Product Cost is hidden</li>
<li>Product Price is hidden for vendor rebate products</li>
<li>unable to delete any products</li>
<li>Product serial number is hidden</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>Restricted View Only #2</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>has access to the do not order field, see screenshot below for other options.</li>
</ul>
<p><span style="color: #0000ff;"><strong>NOTE</strong></span>: <strong><em>In the tables below, each table </em></strong><em><strong>represents how the inventory security setting affects a particular product type</strong></em></p>
<p><em><strong>For example: If you want to see how Restricted View Only #2 will affect a users ability to interact with Non-Stocked products find the Non-Stocked Product Security picture below, find the Security Setting across the top of the picture, and use the grid to find how that security setting affects each option on the Inventory Screen.</strong></em></p>

<h3><a id="Regular Product Security  RQ v5.9 and later"></a>Regular Product Security - RQ v5.9 and later</h3>
<table style="width: 60%;" border="2" width="830" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"><colgroup> <col /> <col /> <col /> <col /> <col /> <col /> </colgroup>

<td style="height: 15px; width: 233px; background-color: #afafaf;" height="15"><strong>Field</strong></td>
<td style="width: 87px; background-color: #afafaf;"><strong>Full Access</strong></td>

<h3><a id="Non Revenue Product Security"></a>Non-Revenue Product Security</h3>
<table style="width: 60%;" border="2" width="817" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"><colgroup> <col /> <col /> <col /> <col /> <col /> <col /> </colgroup>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td style="height: 15px; width: 241px; background-color: #afafaf;" height="15"><strong>Field</strong></td>
<td style="width: 71px; background-color: #afafaf;"><strong>Full Access</strong></td>
<td style="width: 109px; background-color: #afafaf;"><strong>Restricted Access</strong></td>

<p><a id="Inventory_Inventory_Removal"></a><u><strong>Inventory: Inventory Removal</strong></u></p>
<p><em>Inventory Console | Tools | Inventory Removal</em></p>
<p><em><strong>Full Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>provides all functions available to this screen</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>No Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>access is denied</li>
<li>message will display, "You do not have security clearance"</li>
</ul>
<p>For details on <strong>Full Access</strong> see <a href="https://support.iqmetrix.com/hc/en-us/articles/229069788-Inventory-Console#Inventory_Removal"> Manually Adjusting Inventory</a></p>
<p><a id="Inventory_Min_Max_Pricing_Adjustments"></a><u><strong>Inventory: Min/Max Pricing Adjustments</strong></u></p>
<p><em>Reports Console | Inventory | Min/Max Pricing Adjustments</em></p>
<p><em><strong>Full Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>view/edit all results</li>
<li>set <strong>Sale Begin Date</strong></li>
<li>set <strong>Sale End Date</strong></li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>Assigned Locations Only</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>view/edit results for own locations only</li>
<li>set <strong>Sale Begin Date</strong> for assigned location(s)</li>
<li>set <strong>Sale End Date</strong> for assigned location(s)</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>View Only</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>view all results</li>
<li>unable to edit</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>No Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>access is denied</li>
<li>message will display, "You do not have security clearance"</li>
</ul>
<p>For details on <strong>Full Access</strong> see <a href="https://support.iqmetrix.com/hc/en-us/articles/228830487#Min_Max_Pricing_Adjustments">Min/Max Pricing Adjustments</a></p>

<p><a id="Inventory_New_Count_Sheet"></a><u><strong>Inventory: New Count Sheet</strong></u></p>
<p><em>Inventory Console | Count Sheet | New Count Sheet</em></p>
<p><em><strong>Full Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>create count sheet for any location</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>Restricted - Count Your Own Location</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>create count sheet for own location only</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>Restricted - Blind Count Your Own Location</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>create blind count for own location</li>
<li><strong>Preview </strong>button is disabled</li>
<li><strong>Print </strong>button is disabled</li>
<li><strong>Email</strong> button is disabled</li>
<li><strong>Serial Number</strong> column is hidden</li>
<li><strong>In Stock</strong> column is hidden</li>
<li><strong>Variance </strong>column is hidden</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>No Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>access is denied</li>
<li>message will display, "You do not have security clearance"</li>
</ul>
<p><span style="color: #0000ff;"><strong>NOTE</strong></span>: <em><strong>Blind Count</strong> security will affect users counting inventory:</em></p>
<p>When the counter has a <strong>Blind Count</strong> security level the Tracking Number (ESN/IMEI/Serial Number) will not be displayed for them and they will have to scan in the tracking number for each serialized product</p>
<p>For details on <strong>Full Access</strong> see <a href="https://support.iqmetrix.com/hc/en-us/articles/229069788-Inventory-Console#Physical_Inventory_Count_Overview_and_FAQ">Physical Inventory Count</a></p>

</ul>
<p><strong><em>By Product Only</em></strong></p>
<div>
<ul>
<li>missing security clearance error when a <strong>By Invoice</strong> or <strong>Percentage of Invoice</strong> coupon is first selected</li>
<li><strong>Cancel</strong> is enabled</li>
<li><strong>Delete</strong> is disabled when a <strong>By Invoice</strong> or <strong>Percentage of Invoice</strong> coupon is selected</li>
<li>editing is disallowed when a <strong>By Invoice</strong> or <strong>Percentage of Invoice</strong> coupon is selected</li>
<li><strong>Create</strong> is enabled</li>
<li><strong>Save</strong> is disabled when a <strong>By Invoice</strong> or <strong>Percentage of Invoice</strong> coupon is selected</li>
<li><strong>Discount Method</strong> dropdown is missing <strong>By Invoice</strong> and <strong>Percentage of Invoice</strong> options</li>
<li><strong>Create Similar</strong> is disabled when a <strong>By Invoice</strong> or <strong>Percentage of Invoice</strong> coupon is selected</li>
<li>run <strong>Coupon History</strong> report</li>
</ul>
</div>
<p><em><strong>View Only</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>most buttons are disabled</li>
<li>can run <strong>Coupon History</strong> report</li>
<li>can <strong>Print Labels</strong></li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>No Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>access is denied</li>
<li>message will display, "You do not have security clearance"</li>
</ul>
<p>For details on <strong>Full Access</strong> see <a href="https://support.iqmetrix.com/hc/en-us/articles/229127388-Settings-Sales#Coupon_Setup">Coupon Setup</a></p>

<p><a id="POS_Invoices"></a><u><strong>POS: Invoices</strong></u></p>
<p><em>Sales Console (Quick Sale or New Sale)</em></p>
<p><u>Sale Functions include:</u></p>
<ul>
<li>access to Refund, Bill Pay / Deposit, integration partners, etc. on the toolbar at the top</li>
<li>access to product picker and add products</li>
<li>access to Notes and Charity portion</li>
<li>Cost button to show Cost on the left of invoice quanity.</li>
<li>access Suggestive Sell List and edit product quantity, product unit price, tax and remove the product in Invoice item control</li>
<li>add and remove the customer</li>
<li>access Extra charge, Coupon, Tax and Check out</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>Full Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>access all sale functions</li>
<li>view cost</li>
</ul>
<p><span style="color: #0000ff;"><strong>NOTE:</strong></span> <em>Floor Level Pricing does not affect this security level</em></p>
<p><span style="color: #0000ff;"><strong>NOTE:</strong></span> <em>if the Manager Override feature is turned on, only this security level will be able to perform overrides</em></p>
<p><em><strong>Show Rebate Prices, Hide Cost</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>access all sale functions</li>
<li>view rebate prices</li>
<li>unable to view cost</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>Hide Rebate Prices, Show Cost</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>access all sale functions</li>
<li>unable to view rebate prices</li>
<li>view cost</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>Hide Rebate Prices, Hide Cost</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>access all sale functions</li>
<li>unable to view rebate prices</li>
<li>unable to view cost</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>No Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>access is denied</li>
<li>message will display, "You do not have security clearance" when <strong>New Sale</strong> is clicked or customer is chosen</li>
</ul>
<p><span style="color: #0000ff;"><strong>NOTE:</strong></span> <em>Price Editing at the point of sale</em></p>
<ul>
<li><em>the ability to edit the selling price of a SKU at the point of sale is a product attribute, not a security setting</em></li>
<li><em>a product is either discountable or it is not</em></li>
<li><em>see <a href="https://support.iqmetrix.com/hc/en-us/articles/229070368-Inventory-Products#Creating_a_new_Regular_Product">Creating a New Regular Product</a> for details of the discountable functionality</em></li>
</ul>
<p>For details on <strong>Full Access</strong> see <a href="https://support.iqmetrix.com/hc/en-us/articles/229063468-Customer-Profile#Customer_Profile_Sales">Sales Tab</a></p>

<li>view cost and gross profit on sales order products</li>

<li>unable to view cost and gross profit on sales order products</li>
<li>discounting of sales order products is restricted by minimum &amp; maximum price of the product (except with manager override)​</li>
</ul>

<li>message will display, "You do not have security clearance"</li>

<p><a id="POS_Refunds"></a><u><strong>POS: Refunds</strong></u></p>
<p><em>Sales Console | Refund</em></p>
<p><em><strong>Full Access </strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>perform refunds and swaps without limitation</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>Refund Related Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>refund and swap related products on the <strong>Find Invoice To Refund</strong> screen</li>
<li>the view automatically selects/deselects all related products when a product is selected to be refunded/swapped</li>
</ul>
<p><span style="color: #0000ff;"><strong>NOTE</strong></span>: <em>this is to avoid the user swapping only one product from the invoice, then removing the swap product once on the invoice screen, leaving only the one item to be refunded</em></p>
<p><em><strong>Override &amp; Refund Related</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>refund and swap related products on the <strong>Find Invoice to Refund</strong> screen if manager overrides are enabled and they have a valid manager override</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>No Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>unable to perform refunds (if manager override is enabled, prompt for override will appear at checkout)</li>
</ul>
<p>For details on <strong>Full Access</strong> see <a href="https://support.iqmetrix.com/hc/en-us/articles/229127008-Sales-Console#Refunding_Swapping_A_Sale">Refunding/Swapping A Sale</a></p>

<li>del<span style="line-height: 1.6em;">ete records</span></li>
<li>rate plan rebates tab is hidden</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>No Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>unable to view records</li>
<li>message will display, "You do not have security clearance"</li>
</ul>

<p><a id="POS_Update_Sales_Order"></a><u><strong>POS: Update Sales Order</strong></u></p>
<p><em>Customers Console | Customer Profile | History</em></p>
<p><em>Customers Console | Customer Profile | Sales</em></p>
<p><em><strong>Show Rebate Prices, Show Cost</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>view prices of vendor rebates on the order</li>
<li>view cost and gross profit on sales order products</li>
<li>unrestricted discounting of sales order products</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>Show Rebate Prices, Hide Cost</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>view prices of vendor rebates on the order</li>
<li>unable to view cost and gross profit on sales order products</li>
<li>discounting of sales order products is restricted by minimum and maximum price of the product (except with manager override)</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>Hide Rebate Prices, Show Cost</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>view cost and gross profit on sales order products</li>
<li>unable to view prices of vendor rebates on the order</li>
<li>discounting of sales order products is restricted by minimum and maximum price of the product (except with manager override)</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>Hide Rebate Prices, Hide Cost</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>unable to view prices of vendor rebates on the order</li>
<li>unable to view cost and gross profit on sales order products</li>
<li>discounting of sales order products is restricted by minimum &amp; maximum price of the product (except with manager override)​</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>No Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>access is denied</li>
<li>message will display, "You do not have security clearance"</li>
</ul>
<p><span style="color: #0000ff;"><strong>NOTE</strong></span>: <em>at stores with <strong>Store-In-Store</strong> flow enabled, <strong>No Access</strong> is treated as <strong>Hide Rebate Prices, Show Cost</strong></em></p>
<p>For details on <strong>Full Access</strong> see <a href="https://support.iqmetrix.com/hc/en-us/articles/229127008-Sales-Console#Updating_or_Completing_a_Sales_Order">Sales Orders</a></p>

<h1><a id="PPS_Payment_Processing_Settings_Security_Settings"></a>PPS (Payment Processing Settings) Security Settings</h1>
<p><a href="#PPS_Manual_Entry">PPS: Manual Entry</a><br /> <a href="#PPS_Override_AVS">PPS: Override AVS</a><br /> <a href="#PPS_Override_CVV">PPS: Override CVV</a><br /> <a href="#PPS_Override_Terminal_ID">PPS: Override Terminal ID</a><br /> <a href="#PPS_Phone_Authorization">PPS: Phone Authorization</a><br /> <a href="#PPS_Refund_To_Non_Credit_Card">PPS: Refund To Non Credit Card</a></p>
<p><a id="PPS_Manual_Entry"></a><u><strong>PPS: Manual Entry</strong></u></p>
<p><em>Sales Console | Sale</em></p>
<p><em><strong>Full Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>manual entry will be an option at the point of tender on payment types with <strong>Require Credit Card Authorization</strong> checked</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>Allow on Device Only </strong></em><span style="color: #0000ff;"><strong>- as of RQ v5.14</strong></span></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p>option to do manual entry on device will be displayed, but not the option to do manual entry in RQ, on payment types with <strong>Require Credit Card Authorization</strong> checked</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>Allow From RQ Only </strong></em><span style="color: #0000ff;"><strong>- as of RQ v5.14</strong></span></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p>option to do manual entry in RQ will be displayed, but not the option to do manual entry on device, on payment types with <strong>Require Credit Card Authorization</strong> checked</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>No Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>manual entry will not be an option at the point of tender on payment types with <strong>Require Credit Card </strong><strong>Authorization</strong> checked</li>
</ul>
<p>For details on <strong>Full Access</strong> see <a href="https://support.iqmetrix.com/hc/en-us/articles/229127048-Sales-and-Refunds#Take_a_credit_card_payment">Creating A New Sale</a></p>
<p><a id="PPS_Override_AVS"></a><u><strong>PPS: Override AVS</strong></u></p>
<p><em>​​Security is enforced during manual entry of credit card payment without AVS values</em></p>
<p><em><strong>Full Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>authorize transactions without AVS values</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>No Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>require an override from a user with <strong>Full Access </strong>to authorize transactions without AVS values​</li>
</ul>
<p>When processing a payment using a <strong>Manual Card Entry</strong> method and the user does not have permission to submit payment without AVS it will be asked if they want to do <strong>Manager Override</strong></p>
<p>If <strong>Manager Override</strong> is successful, RQ will continue with processing payment</p>
<p>If <strong>Manager Override</strong> is not successful, user will be taken back to card entry screen</p>
<p>If the user has permission to submit payment without AVS, RQ will continue with processing payment</p>
<p><strong>Manager Override</strong> need to be done for each <strong>Manual Entry</strong>, regardless if the Credit Card type is the same</p>
<p>For details on <strong>Full Access</strong> see <a href="https://support.iqmetrix.com/hc/en-us/articles/229127048-Sales-and-Refunds#Take_a_credit_card_payment">Creating A New Sale</a></p>
<p><a id="PPS_Override_CVV"></a><u><strong>PPS: Override CVV</strong></u></p>
<p><em>Security is enforced during manual entry of credit card payment without a CVV number. This setting is applicable to Manual Entry from RQ only. CVV is always required when manually entering through the Payment Device.</em></p>
<p><em><strong>Full Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>authorize transactions without CVV values</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>No Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>require an override from a user with Full Access to authorize transactions without CVV values​</li>
</ul>
<p>When processing a payment using a <strong>Manual Card Entry</strong> method and the user does not have permission to submit payment without CVV it will be asked if they want to do <strong>Manager Override</strong></p>
<p>If <strong>Manager Override</strong> is successful, RQ will continue with processing payment</p>
<p>If <strong>Manager Override</strong> is not successful, user will be taken back to card entry screen</p>
<p>If the user has permission to submit payment without CVV, RQ will continue with processing payment</p>
<p><strong>Manager Override</strong> need to be done for each <strong>Manual Entry</strong>, regardless if the Credit Card type is the same</p>
<p>For details on <strong>Full Access</strong> see <a href="https://support.iqmetrix.com/hc/en-us/articles/229127048-Sales-and-Refunds#Take_a_credit_card_payment">Creating A New Sale</a></p>
<p><a id="PPS_Override_Terminal_ID"></a><u><strong>PPS: Override Terminal ID</strong></u></p>
<p><em>Settings Console | Workstation Settings | Payment Integration | [provider]</em></p>
<p><em><strong>Full Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>override the terminal ID in <strong>Settings Console | Workstation Settings | Payment Integration</strong></li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>No Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>unable to change the terminal ID</li>
</ul>
<p>For details on <strong>Full Access</strong> see <a href="https://support.iqmetrix.com/hc/en-us/articles/228837827-Settings-Workstation-Settings#Payment_Integration">Workstation Settings</a></p>
<p><a id="PPS_Phone_Authorization"></a><u><strong>PPS: Phone Authorization</strong></u></p>
<p><em>Sales Console | Sale</em></p>
<p><em><strong>Full Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>able to do a phone authorization when needed</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>No Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>will be prompted for an override when attempting a phone authorization</li>
</ul>
<p>For details on <strong>Full Access</strong> see <a href="https://support.iqmetrix.com/hc/en-us/articles/229127008-Sales-Console#Phone_Authorization">Phone Authorization</a></p>
<p><a id="PPS_Refund_To_Non_Credit_Card"></a><u><strong>PPS: Refund To Non Credit Card</strong></u></p>
<p><em>Sales Console | Refund</em></p>
<p><em><strong>Full Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>refund to non credit card payment types when the original sale used a credit card</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>No Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>unable to refund to non credit card payment types when the original sale used a credit card</li>
</ul>
<p>For details on <strong>Full Access</strong> see <a href="https://support.iqmetrix.com/hc/en-us/articles/229127008-Sales-Console#Refunding_Swapping_A_Sale">Refunding/Swapping A Sale</a></p>

<h1><a id="Purchase_Order_Security_Settings"></a><strong>Purchase Order Security Settings</strong></h1>
<p><a href="#Purchase_Order_Complete_Purchase_Order">Purchase Order: Complete Purchase Order</a><br /> <a href="#Purchase_Order_Correct_Receiving_Invoice">Purchase Order: Correct Receiving Invoice</a><br /> <a href="#Purchase_Order_New_Purchase_Order">Purchase Order: New Purchase Order</a><br /> <a href="#Purchase_Order_Order_Policy​​">Purchase Order: Order Policy​​</a><br /> <a href="#Purchase_Order_PO_Mass_Complete">Purchase Order: PO Mass Complete</a><br /> <a href="#Purchase_Order_Receive_Purchase_Order">Purchase Order: Receive Purchase Order</a><br /> <a href="#Purchase_Order_Receive_Purchase_Order_Edit_Products_Ordered">Purchase Order: Receive Purchase Order(Edit Products Ordered)</a><br /> <a href="#Purchase_Order_Reconcile_Receiving_Invoices">Purchase Order: Reconcile Receiving Invoices</a><br /> <a href="#Purchase_Order_Uncommit_Purchase_Order">Purchase Order: Uncommit Purchase Order</a><br /> <a href="#Purchase_Order_Update_Purchase_Order">Purchase Order: Update Purchase Order</a></p>
<p><a id="Purchase_Order_Complete_Purchase_Order"></a><u><strong>Purchase Order: Complete Purchase Order</strong></u></p>
<p><em>Inventory Console | Purchase Orders tab</em></p>
<p><em><strong>Full Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>if access to <strong>PO: Mass Complete</strong> is set to <strong>Full Access</strong> mass complete using <strong>Completed Selected</strong></li>
<li>prompts with <strong>All items have been fully received, would you like to complete this PO?</strong></li>
<li><strong>Completed</strong> checkbox on PO is enabled</li>
<li>complete without receiving everything</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>Auto Complete</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>hides the prompt <strong>All items have been fully received, would you like to complete this PO?</strong></li>
<li>if fully received, PO will automatically be considered complete</li>
<li>unable to complete a PO manually (with the check box)</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>No Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li><strong>Completed</strong> checkbox on PO is hidden</li>
<li>receiving all items on PO does not complete it</li>
</ul>
<p>For details on <strong>Full Access</strong> see <a href="https://support.iqmetrix.com/hc/en-us/articles/229069788-Inventory-Console#Purchase_Order_Overview">Purchase Orders</a></p>

<p><a id="Purchase_Order_New_Purchase_Order"></a><u><strong>Purchase Order: New Purchase Order</strong></u></p>
<p><em>Inventory Console | Purchase Order | New Purchase Order</em></p>
<p><em><strong>Full Access </strong></em></p>

</ul>

<p><a id="Purchase_Order_Order_Policy​​"></a><u><strong>Purchase Order: Order Policy</strong></u></p>

<li>create a purchase order where cost exceeds the maximum defined in <strong>Vendor Setup | Order Policy tab</strong></li>
</ul>
<p><em style="line-height: 1.6em;"><strong>No Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>requires override from <strong>Full Access</strong> user ​to create a purchase order where cost is below the minimum defined in <strong>Vendor Setup | Order Policy tab</strong></li>
<li>requires override from <strong>Full Access</strong> user to create a purchase order where cost exceeds the maximum defined in <strong>Vendor Setup | Order Policy tab</strong></li>
</ul>
<p>For details on <strong>Full Access</strong> see <a href="https://support.iqmetrix.com/hc/en-us/articles/228838047-Settings-Inventory#Order_Policy">Purchase Orders</a></p>

<p><a id="Purchase_Order_Receive_Purchase_Order"></a><u><strong>Purchase Order: Receive Purchase Order</strong></u></p>

<li>see unit cost in <strong>Products Received To Date</strong> grid</li>
<li>see total cost in <strong>Products Received To Date</strong> grid</li>
<li>use <strong>Receive All</strong> button</li>
<li>edit costs in columns</li>
<li>see costs in the <strong>Receiving Invoice Report</strong></li>
<li>see <strong>Total Unit Cost</strong>, <strong>Unit Cost</strong>, <strong>Total Paid</strong> when printing POs</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>Allow Receive All, Show Cost, No Editing Cost</strong></em></p>

<li>see total cost in <strong>Products Ordered</strong> grid</li>
<li>see old cost in <strong>Products Received Today</strong> grid</li>
<li>see new cost in <strong>Products Received Today</strong> grid</li>
<li>see unit cost in <strong>Products Received To Date</strong> grid</li>
<li>see total cost in <strong>Products Received To Date</strong> grid​</li>
<li>use <strong>Receive All</strong> button</li>
<li>unable to edit costs in columns</li>
<li>see costs in the <strong>Receiving Invoice Report</strong></li>
<li>see <strong>Total Unit Cost</strong>, <strong>Unit Cost</strong>, <strong>Total Paid </strong>when printing POs</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>Hide Receive All</strong></em></p>

<li>see old cost in <strong>Products Received Today</strong> grid</li>
<li>see new cost in <strong>Products Received Today</strong> grid</li>
<li>see unit cost in <strong>Products Received To Date</strong> grid</li>
<li>see total cost in <strong>Products Received To Date</strong> grid​</li>
<li>unable to edit costs in columns</li>
<li>see <strong>Total Unit Cost</strong>, <strong>Unit Cost</strong>, <strong>Total Paid </strong>when printing POs</li>
</ul>

</ul>
<p><em><strong>No Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>access is denied</li>
</ul>

<p><a id="Purchase_Order_Receive_Purchase_Order_Edit_Products_Ordered"></a><u><strong>Purchase Order: Receive Purchase Order (Edit Products Ordered)</strong></u></p>
<p><em>Inventory Console | Purchase Orders tab</em></p>
<p><em><strong>Full Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>delete products</li>
<li>edit products</li>
<li><strong>Add Ordered Product</strong> to grid is visible</li>
<li><strong>Ordered Product</strong> identifier is visible</li>
<li><strong>Get Ordered Product</strong> is visible</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>Edit Products Ordered</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>delete products</li>
<li>edit products</li>
<li><strong>Add Ordered Product</strong> to grid is hidden</li>
<li><strong>Ordered Product</strong> identifier is hidden</li>
<li><strong>Get Ordered Product</strong> is hidden</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>No Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>unable to delete products</li>
<li>unable to edit products</li>
<li><strong>Add Ordered Product</strong> to grid is hidden</li>
<li><strong>Ordered Product</strong> identifier is hidden</li>
<li><strong>Get Ordered Product</strong> is hidden</li>
</ul>
<p>For details on <strong>Full Access</strong> see <a href="https://support.iqmetrix.com/hc/en-us/articles/229069788-Inventory-Console#Receive_Purchase_Order">Purchase Orders</a></p>

<li>fingerprint override checkbox is enabled</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>View Only</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>access workstation fingerprint scanner setup</li>
<li>fingerprint override checkbox is disabled</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>No Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>unable to access workstation fingerprint scanner setup</li>
<li>option is not visible in Settings Console</li>
<li><strong>Settings Console</strong> is still accessible if access is granted to other workstation settings, company settings and/or integration settings</li>
<li><strong>Settings Console</strong> is no longer accessible if access is taken away for workstation, company and integration settings</li>
</ul>
<p>For details on <strong>Full Access</strong> see <a href="https://support.iqmetrix.com/hc/en-us/articles/228837827#Fingerprint_Scanner">Workstation Settings</a></p>
<p><a id="Workstation_General"></a><u><strong>Workstation: General</strong></u></p>
<p><em>Settings Console | Workstation Settings | General</em></p>
<p><em><strong>Full Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>view and edit workstation general setup</li>
<li>set workstation default location at login</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>View Only</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>view workstation general setup</li>
<li>unable to set workstation default location at login</li>
</ul>
<p><em><strong>No Access</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>unable to view workstation general setup</li>
<li>option is not visible in <strong>Settings Console</strong></li>
</ul>
<ul>
<li>unable to set workstation default location at login</li>
<li><strong>Settings Console</strong> is still accessible if access is granted to other workstation settings, company settings and/or integration settings</li>
<li><strong>Settings Console</strong> is no longer accessible if access is taken away for workstation, company and integration settings</li>
</ul>
<p>For details on <strong>Full Access</strong> see <a href="https://support.iqmetrix.com/hc/en-us/articles/228837827#General">Workstation Settings</a></p>
